<div id="review_1987182325" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1987182325" />
    <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries"><img alt="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557144778p2/15335689.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1987182325?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries">destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=the-best-of-the-best">the-best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=otp">otp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=found-families">found-families</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1987182325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4752577634747196448"><blockquote>#1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1858462459' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Raven Boys</a> ★★★★★ <br/>#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1987182325' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dream Thieves</a> ★★★★★<br/>#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1868122409' rel='nofollow noopener'>Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a> ★★★★★<br/>#4 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1837779500' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Raven King</a> ★★★★★<br/>#4.5 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2311292720' rel='nofollow noopener'>Opal</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br/><b>“And Ronan was everything that was left: molten eyes and a smile made for war.”</b> <br/><br/>This review took me way too long to write, because it was just so hard to compile my feelings for this book into actual <i>words on a screen</i>. I paced myself and went through this book so slowly, because I couldn't stand not to savor it. It was easily one of the best books I've read all year, and has made </span>
  <span id="freeText4752577634747196448" style="display:none"><blockquote>#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1858462459" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a> ★★★★★ <br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1987182325" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a> ★★★★★<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1868122409" rel="nofollow noopener">Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a> ★★★★★<br />#4 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1837779500" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven King</a> ★★★★★<br />#4.5 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2311292720" rel="nofollow noopener">Opal</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br /><b>“And Ronan was everything that was left: molten eyes and a smile made for war.”</b> <br /><br />This review took me way too long to write, because it was just so hard to compile my feelings for this book into actual <i>words on a screen</i>. I paced myself and went through this book so slowly, because I couldn't stand not to savor it. It was easily one of the best books I've read all year, and has made this one of my favorite series of all time. <br /><br /><b>“It was mint and memories and the past and the future and she felt as if she’d done this before and already she longed to do it again.”</b><br /><br />There is <i>so much</i> character development with my sweet babies Blue and Gansey, and they just broke my heart a million times over and re-mended it every time. I love them both so much and I love their interactions together and there is just this <i>one freaking scene</i> that I have probably reread six times now because I can't get enough of it and I'M TRYING NOT TO SPOIL THIS BOOK FOR YOU GUYS BUT OH MY <b>GOD</b>.<br /><br /><b>“In that moment, Blue was a little in love with all of them.<br />Their magic. Their quest. Their awfulness and strangeness.<br />Her raven boys.”</b><br /><br />Then, of course, there are Adam and Noah, who are so far my least favorite Raven boys (don't throw anything at me!), but I do still love them <b>so much I can't stand it</b>. Adam is so full of heartache and rage and hurt, and then poor little Noah is the epitome of a cinnamon roll and I just want to hug him and fix everything. 💔 Can we talk about the Blue/Noah scene in Monmouth? KILLED ME DEAD.<br /><br /><b>“I am being perfectly fucking civil.”</b><br /><br />And then... there's <i>
  <b>Ronan</b>
</i>. This felt like Ronan's book, first and foremost, and I loved every single word on every single page that involved him. He's such a brilliant, badass, lovable character and the development that he underwent in this installment was mind-blowing. I loved learning about his dreams, and his family, and the soft little heart tucked under all that anger and stubble and ink.<br /><br />On top of these lovable little delights of my heart, you've got more fun shenanigans with Maura and the psychics, breathtaking antics with a few morally <b>
  <i>gray</i>
</b> characters (heh, get it?), deliciously creepy Cabeswater adventures, and a hell of a lot of magic. Through it all, Maggie's writing is so stunning and fun, and these characters made me want to live in Henrietta just to watch it all unfold.<br /><br />If you enjoyed <i>The Raven Boys</i>, you positively <b>
  <i>must</i>
</b> continue the series. If you haven't picked this series up at all yet, well... what are you waiting for?!<br /><br />You can find this review (and more) on my <a href="https://howlinglibraries.com/2017/09/24/thedreamthieves/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4752577634747196448" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1719467349" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3696661202184877669"><b>5/5 <i>I love Ronan so goddamn much</i> stars</b><br/><br/><b>Pre-Dream Thieves Me:</b> Okay, there is no way I could possibly love Ronan Lynch anymore than I do now.<br/><br/><b>Post-Dream Thieves Me:</b> Think again, bitch.<br/><br/>I've written and re-written this review so many times now, that I've just accepted I'll never be able to put into words how much I love this series, and how much I loved this book. So I wrote a gif-review instead. Enjoy.<br/><br/><b>This book:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398095999ra/9367437.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471907675ra/20123387.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Adam:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906791ra/20123305.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Blue:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385802234ra/7231807.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ronan and Adam:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420781351ra/13261471.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Blue</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3696661202184877669" style="display:none"><b>5/5 <i>I love Ronan so goddamn much</i> stars</b><br><br><b>Pre-Dream Thieves Me:</b> Okay, there is no way I could possibly love Ronan Lynch anymore than I do now.<br><br><b>Post-Dream Thieves Me:</b> Think again, bitch.<br><br>I've written and re-written this review so many times now, that I've just accepted I'll never be able to put into words how much I love this series, and how much I loved this book. So I wrote a gif-review instead. Enjoy.<br><br><b>This book:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398095999ra/9367437.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img <div id="review_1718760970" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1718760970" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1718760970?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1718760970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5246034722209937627"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“While I'm gone, dream me the world. Something new for every night.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>I feel like I just woke up from a dream.</b> Slightly <b>disoriented</b>, like I can't separate reality from fiction. Like I can't remember the exact context of this bizarre dream but I can recollect scattered images and emotions. <b>Bliss. Anger. Agony. Pain.</b><br/><b>Love.</b> For this series and its raw, complicated and <i>real</i> characters.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “It was mint and memories and the past and the future and she felt as if she’d done this before an</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5246034722209937627" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“While I'm gone, dream me the world. Something new for every night.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>I feel like I just woke up from a dream.</b> Slightly <b>disoriented</b>, like I can't separate reality from fiction. Like I can't remember the exact context of this bizarre dream but I can recollect scattered images and emotions. <b>Bliss. Anger. Agony. Pain.</b><br><b>Love.</b> For this series and its raw, complicated and <i>real</i> characters.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “It was mint and memories and the past and the future and she felt as if she’d done this before and already she longed to do it again.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17347389.The_Dream_Thieves__The_Raven_Cycle___2_" title="The Dream Thieves (The Raven Cycle, #2) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a> is more focused on Ronan's history, his past, his secrets and his terrifying ability of pulling things out of his dreams. At the same time, Adam struggles to come to terms with the sacrifice he made, Gansey continues his relentless search of the long dead Welsh king and Blue realizes that heart is a traitorous thing and you can't choose who you fall in love with. When a mysterious man appears and strange<i>r</i> paranormal activity strikes their little town, Blue and her raven boys must solve the riddles of their abilities and the ley lines and discover what they're looking for before it is too late. Before someone else does.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“All of us have secrets in our lives. We’re keepers or keptfrom, players or played. Secrets and cockroaches — that’s what will be left at the end of it all.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17347389.The_Dream_Thieves__The_Raven_Cycle___2_" title="The Dream Thieves (The Raven Cycle, #2) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dream Thieves</a>, but not as much as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17675462.The_Raven_Boys__The_Raven_Cycle___1_" title="The Raven Boys (The Raven Cycle, #1) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a>. I was overwhelmed with a constant <b>restlessness</b>, I almost skipped sentences and pages because I wanted something <i>more</i>, something <i>else</i> to happen but I can't pinpoint what that was. Perhaps I got tired from the frequent switch between dreams and reality, and I ended up <b>a tad unsatisfied</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470326566ra/19915438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“In that moment, Blue was a little in love with all of them. Their magic. Their quest. Their awfulness and strangeness. Her raven boys.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Despite this uneasy feeling though, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1330292.Maggie_Stiefvater" title="Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">Maggie Stiefvater</a>'s writing didn't lose its <b>mystical</b> and <b>seductive</b> touch. <b>This book's greatest asset was that it explored more thoroughly the relationships between the characters and their personalities</b>, their inner battles and desires and needs. It explained Ronan's hatred against the world, it uncovered the secrets he safeguarded for so long and I fell for his wounded, more vulnerable side. Adam on the contrary became more unpredictable. I can't shake the notion that he is <b>jealous</b> of Gansey and that's the source of his bitterness. He is changing, I can see that he's changing and I hope that he'll understand how awful he has been to Gansey who only wanted to help him. My sweet, dear Gansey, whose wilder, boyish side is equally intriguing with his scholarly one.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I wish you could be kissed, Jane,' he said. 'Because I would beg just one off you. Under all this.' He flailed an arm toward the stars.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470341411ra/19917165.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There is no doubt <i>my</i> love, <i>their</i> love will hurt. But their connection, their stolen moments, the longing, they made my toes curl and my heart beat rapidly, sending warmth to every single cell of my body. I am scared and excited at the same time, but I hope, hope, hope.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Rex corvus. Parate regis corvi.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>The Raven Cycle is a bewitching tale</b>, and I'm off to start <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17378508.Blue_Lily__Lily_Blue__The_Raven_Cycle___3_" title="Blue Lily, Lily Blue (The Raven Cycle, #3) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">Blue Lily, Lily Blue</a>, because staying away from Blue and her raven boys is impossible. When I end this series, I'll probably need therapy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5246034722209937627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1810256929" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1810256929" />
    <a title="jess " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40929181-jess"><img alt="jess " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605207720p2/40929181.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1810256929?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jess " class="user" itemprop="url" name="jess " href="/user/show/40929181-jess">jess </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1810256929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9430428922396743394"><i>In that moment, Blue was a little in love with all of them. Their magic. Their quest, Their awfulness and strangeness. Her raven boys</i><br/><br/>This book was something out of a dream. Reading this felt like developing a crush. When you just look at something/someone and it just feels <i>right</i>. And as time goes on, you continue to love that person more and more. Falling in love with their nervous mannerisms and they way they speak. Reading this was like continuously falling in love with someone, deeper and dee</span>
  <span id="freeText9430428922396743394" style="display:none"><i>In that moment, Blue was a little in love with all of them. Their magic. Their quest, Their awfulness and strangeness. Her raven boys</i><br><br>This book was something out of a dream. Reading this felt like developing a crush. When you just look at something/someone and it just feels <i>right</i>. And as time goes on, you continue to love that person more and more. Falling in love with their nervous mannerisms and they way they speak. Reading this was like continuously falling in love with someone, deeper and deeper. And oh man, am I ever falling in love with this story.<br><br>I can never express my love enough for these characters. There's something so profound and real about them, that it's almost overwhelming. It's like....I need them to be real. Because they already feel so alive in my mind. <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518538249ra/25052959.gif" alt="Image result for gansey gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Gansey</b> - He is such a nerd. I love him to death. I know I've already gushed about these characters, but reading this book felt like knowing them all over again. Gansey is something so rare and strange and giddy. He can be a little child one minute and the next, a cool, calm adult. Reading from his POV, felt like knowing some sort of a secret because you finally know what he's really thinking and not just seeing his shiny exterior. He reminds me soft butter, and freckles, and warm hands. Honestly, what an awkward lovely weirdo he is.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518538249ra/25052960.gif" alt="Image result for blue sargent gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br><b>Blue</b> - Ugh, this girl is a tiny, raging feminist and I am completely in love with it. Not only does she warm my heart with every clever word she speaks, but she makes me feel like dressing in old band tees and crocheting myself some leggings. I adore her friendship with Noah. It has to be one of the most pure things in the entire book and it makes me feel sleepy and warm and nostalgic for when I was a kid when everything was soft laughter and warm hugs. Also Blue's relationship with her mom and her relatives just makes me feel so soft and happy. I love her family so much.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518538249ra/25052963.gif" alt="Image result for ronan lynch gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Ronan</b> - Ronan is like a toasted marshmallow. On the outside, he's a little bit tough but when you get through that, he's really just a mushy emotional mess. Everything he does is done so impulsively, not really thinking about what'll happen next, and boy can I relate. Reading about him made me want to be reckless and shave my head and have the best sense of humor in the world. Also, the way he was so so protective of Matthew<i>(the cutest little cupcake in the entire universe)</i>made me super duper happy. I love his relationship with him and I love Matthew so much that sometimes it physically hurts. There's something about Ronan, that when he feels something, you feel it too. My insides are crying for this boy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518538249ra/25052961.gif" alt="Image result for adam parrish gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Adam</b> - Ah Adam, our troubled, troubled young man. Reading about Adam was like sitting at the bottom of a swimming pool where everything is softer and floaty and less often. Everything felt almost like a blur with him. I just felt everything so much when reading from his POV. And I love him with every fiber of my being but sometimes he almost frustrated me. He never accepts help from people. And while I perfectly understand why <i>(and the reasons make me cry in 72 different languages)</i>, I've also realized that sometimes accepting help doesn't mean you're weak. It just means that you know yourself well enough to understand that sometimes you can't do everything alone. Anyway, I cry for Adam Parrish several times in a hour and I will protect him with every piece of my heart.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518538249ra/25052962.gif" alt="Image result for noah czerny gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Noah</b> - There is no one in this series that makes me feel more child-like and sad-happy than Noah. Every time I think of him, my mind automatically jumps to the word <i>hufflepuff</i>. He's fluffy and kind and just everything I think a hufflepuff is and I adore him with all my soul. Even though I understand why he doesn't get much page-time, I still wish he would be in the book more. <br><br>This book makes me feel exciting and strange and mysterious, like I could find an adventure right where I am. Also it is intriguing as frick?? All those different POVs, I think, really kept me guessing and wanting more. And even though the 1st book is lovely and amazing, there's just....ugh I don't know, <i>something</i> about <i>The Dream Thieves</i> that makes me want to die and become resurrected in Henrietta, Virginia. <i>( Also if Adam and Ronan do not end up together at the end of this, I will feel personally attacked by Maggie and will indeed fite someone)</i><br><br>Anyways, this book is a summertime thunderstorm where everything is dark green and gray and wild and you feel like you could fly away. And I am crushing on it and you should be too.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9430428922396743394" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This was so fucking good. AHhhh so fuc</span>
  <span id="freeText17879476444793941362" style="display:none">This was supposed to be a BR with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/60226508-blue" rel="nofollow noopener">this bitch</a>, but she decided to read without me and then DNF it halfway in because <i>it was too boring</i>. I'm questioning our friendship too. <s>So like, I'm going to force her to finish this and BR the next book with me.</s> <br><br>When I finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17675462.The_Raven_Boys__The_Raven_Cycle___1_" title="The Raven Boys (The Raven Cycle, #1) by Maggie Stiefvater" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Boys</a>, I was left confused and bored and didn't really want to pick up this book because I didn't want to read something that was confusing as fuck and boring as fuck, but HOW WRONG I WAS! This was so fucking good. AHhhh so fucking good, you guys. <b>I officially love Ronan and the Gray Man.</b><br><br><b>Ronan <i>fucking</i> Lynch:</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Everything about him was a warning: If this snake bit you, you had no one to blame but yourself.” <br><br>"Don't fucking swear," Ronan said."<br><br>"I am being perfectly fucking civil"<br><br>"Noah slouched in. In a wounded tone, he said, "He threw me out the window!"<br>Ronan's voice sang out from behind his closed door: "You're already dead!” </i>
</b><br><br>I finally understand why everyone is so crazy over this beautiful little fucking bastard. I love him so much. He's the best characters in this book. He deserves all the fucking love. He is hilarious as fuck and I can relate so much to him. This fucking kid, I swear. <br><br>So like, since my brain is dysfunctional, I keep on saying Ronan Lynch out loud and this is an <i>actual</i> conversation I had with my sister. <br><br>Me: *stares at Ronan Lynch fanart* Ronan Lynch<br>Sister: Who the fuck is this Ronan Lynch? WHy are you ALWAYS saying RONAN LYNCH?!?!?!?!<br>Me: Child, you don't know who this Lynch is because you never fUCKING READ. <br>Sister: Get a life Sun. <br>Me: dO yOu wAnT tO sTaRt a fIgHt?!<br><br><b>When I found out about Ronan's second secret</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482692250i/21540213.jpg" width="250" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <br>

 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Just fuck me up please. JUST FUCKING KILL ME. I CAN'T TAKE IT AHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH.<br><br><b>Chainsaw:</b><br>Chainsaw is love. <br>Yes, this bird is my fucking favorite, after Ronan of course. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482692851i/21540248._SY540_.jpg" width="600" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Gray Man:</b><br>He's a mysterious hit man. He's a violent little piece of shit. He's a wonderful violent piece of shit. And I ship him so fucking hard with Maura. Maura deserves happiness. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482693466i/21540264._SY540_.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"The Gray Man took the gun from the passenger seat and shot his brother. Twice."</i>
</blockquote><br>This quote makes me really happy. Please don't ask why. Thanks. <br><br><b>Kavinsky:</b><br> <blockquote>
  <i>"Ronan said, 'Life isn't just sex and drugs and cars.'<br>Kavinsky said, 'Mine is.'"</i>
</blockquote><br><i>This</i> little bitch ass fucker. I <i>hate</i> him. I don't understand why everyone likes him??? Sorry, but I don't like this guy. Sure he's funny, but what he did at the end was not cool. AND HE'S A DANGER TO PYNCH, SO NO THANK YOU BIG TIME. :)<br><br>AND HE JUST GETS TO FUCKING SMACK RONAN'S HEAD??? <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and when he died I was so happy, but I have a feeling he's going to come back to life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Overall, the beginning was a bit slow, but the characters were hella funny and lovable and it got way better as I was reading on. I still don't understand shit about the ley lines and Glendower or whatever the plot is. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17879476444793941362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1176064060" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1176064060" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1176064060?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1176064060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2168105319225821513"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i> All of us have secrets in our lives. We’re keepers or kept-from, players or played. Secrets and cockroaches — that’s what will be left at the end of it all.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Blurb:</b> If you could steal things from dreams, what would you take?<br/>Ronan Lynch has secrets. Some he keeps from others. Some he keeps from himself.<br/>One secret: Ronan can bring things out of his dreams.<br/>And sometimes he's not the only one who wants those things.<br/>Ronan is one of the raven boys - a group of friends, practically brothers, searchi</span>
  <span id="freeText2168105319225821513" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i> All of us have secrets in our lives. We’re keepers or kept-from, players or played. Secrets and cockroaches — that’s what will be left at the end of it all.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Blurb:</b> If you could steal things from dreams, what would you take?<br>Ronan Lynch has secrets. Some he keeps from others. Some he keeps from himself.<br>One secret: Ronan can bring things out of his dreams.<br>And sometimes he's not the only one who wants those things.<br>Ronan is one of the raven boys - a group of friends, practically brothers, searching for a dead king named Glendower, who they think is hidden somewhere in the hills by their elite private school, Aglionby Academy. The path to Glendower has long lived as an undercurrent beneath town. But now, like Ronan's secrets, it is beginning to rise to the surface - changing everything in its wake.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443645190i/16388684.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Weird af brilliant book. That’s all I can say.<br><br>I have such an odd relationship with this series. When I first pick up a book <i>(it happened with both TRB and TDT)</i>, I put it away. Maybe I feel it’s too slow or I won’t really care about the new characters but <u>I always end up reading it and loving the shit out of it.</u><br><br>I’m still surprised of how much I care and how much I like almost all the characters. That by itself is a rarity but when you combine likeable characters with actually great characterization, good development and a compelling story, well, you have the keys to success.<br>I can’t say I liked this one better than the first one, maybe I liked it a tiny bit less but that doesn’t mean I didn’t love it.<br><br>So, this second book is mostly about Ronan and Adam. <br><br>We get to know more about how he takes stuff out of his dreams, the complications of it, the risks and how Ronan Lynch’s head works. There’s desperation, angry, regrets, secrets and content. <br><br>In my TRB review I said Ronan was one of my favorite characters and, after this book, he is probably one of my favorites <u>ever.</u> There are so many layers and so many aspect of his persona but, somehow, he still manages to be quite simple.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443645191ra/16388685.gif" width="500" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I got really fucking frustrated with his relationship with Kavisnky but that could be because I absolutely hated Joseph Kavinsky. That little shit was just too much for me and I feel it was also Ronan’s mirror. Like, that could’ve been him if he didn’t have Gansey and the others so I both hated and enjoyed all the scenes where Kavinsky was in. And I rather enjoyed Kavinsky’s innuendos. <br><br>Boy, it was so obvious he was into Ronan.<br><br>There were two particular scenes that made me think (before shit went south) that the only thing Kavinsky wanted was someone to be with.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> With a theatric twist of his hand, he presented his dream object. A pen cap. He twitched his fingers until Ronan handed over the dream-pen.<br>The cap, of course, fit perfectly.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>That was the first time I thought he wanted someone to complete him. Maybe I am reading too much between lines but I don’t think so. As the story goes, well, everything falls into place.<br><br>But there was also this one:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> After a moment, he heard the hood groan as Kavinsky leaned over him. Then he felt the ridged callus of a finger drag slowly over the skin on his back. A slow arc between his shoulder blades, drawing the pattern of his tattoo. Then sliding down his spine, tensing every muscle it moved over.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>There was nothing subtle about the way Kavinsky wanted Ronan and nothing subtle about Ronan’s response, or lack of it.<br><br>I toyed with the idea of Kavinsky getting better but it was a no-go. He wanted to own and be owned by Ronan. He wouldn’t share him but, as much I didn’t like him, I do appreciate his whole role.<br><br>Now, Ronan’s relationship with his brothers is so tricky I still don’t know how to feel.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443645191ra/16388686.gif" width="300" height="214" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He loves Matthew, that’s a sure thing and he hates Declan but I don’t know how much he hates him. Does he hate him enough to kill him one day if it comes to it? Does he hate him enough to stop caring if something happens to him? He was clearly disturbed by Declan being all bruised and he also included him in the will. <br><br>That’s why I don’t know. I know it’ll come a time where Declan’s going to be more involved and I just hope Ronan doesn’t regret his decisions towards his older brother. Whether they’re good or bad.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> Everyone at St. Agnes knew the Lynch brothers didn’t come to church alone.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, let’s talk about Adam.<br><br>I don’t know if I love him or hate him. Well, <i>hate</i> is such a strong word but maybe frustration? Yes! I’m frustrated! Look, I like Adam more than I used to but I still can’t wrap my heart around him. Gosh, I wanna love that guy, I do. I feel like loving Adam Parrish could be so good but he needs to stop directing his anger toward the wrong people. Granted, he doesn’t have many people in his life to decide on whom he’ll be angry at but come on, boy, just stop.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437355517ra/15577102.gif" width="400" height="204" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He needs to level up, to own himself so he can take down the world or something. Adam’s right when it comes to his value: he can do <u>anything</u> he wants but he also has to stop for a second and breathe.<br><br>He has his demons to battle but he’s not alone. Contrary of the way he sees it, he’s not alone and he will never be alone again. Even if they all part ways (seriously, though, can you imagine them going on different ways?) he will never be alone. <br><br>Adam wants, <i>needs,</i> Glendower so badly he can blind himself in the process. But with that been said, I found myself liking this Adam a lot more. He has some clarity that TRB Adam didn’t have and a brand new sense of resolution. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> It was nothing, but it was Adam Parrish’s nothing. How he hated and loved it. How proud he was of it, how wretched it was.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love he’s proud and he wants to do things on his own, it’s what he needs after all that’s happened to him but he still needs to find a way to be proud but also be proud of having friends that would help him and actually accept their help.<br><br>I also liked how he wanted answers from Blue, <i>that was so not the way to get them, though</i>, but I liked that. He did deserve more and he did deserve to know what was on the table. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430799639ra/14764192.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have big hope for Adam but there’s something bothering me. Or maybe not bother but rather confusing the heck outta me. Calla called Ronan <i>Magician</i> but then Adam’s reading showed he was the magician and Persephone also <u>named</u> him that. What’s the truth? Did Calla just call Ronan Magician because Adam’s his fate? After all, Ronan’s the Greywaren. <br><br><b>I’m so digging Adam and Ronan together.</b><br><br>Now, the Gray Man. <br><br>What the actual fuck with the guy?<br><br>At first I thought he was the villain but then he was like not really that but rather a neutral agent and then he was not so neutral after all and then what?<br><br>I was trying my hardest not to care about him because, after he decide he wasn’t going to take Ronan, I was so sure he was going to be killed I didn’t want to invest my feelings on an already dead character.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443645191ra/16388687.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also played with the idea of him being Blue’s father but nope. Maura would’ve known him immediately but I still liked him. He was more complex than I thought he was going to be. And though I liked him enough, I can’t still make a solid idea of him. <br><br>He was afraid of his brother, yet he killed him like he was not the threat I thought he was going to be. <br><br>Calla actually liked him, <i>Calla fucking liked him.</i> And his relationship with Maura was so cute, geez. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> The Gray Man thought of Maura’s smile again. And he thought of the fuss and noise of 300 Fox Way, of Blue’s bright banter, of the tuna fish sandwich at the deli counter, the haunted blue mountains calling him home.<br>He wanted to stay.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Those were, to me, the main characters of this book but I’d like to discuss very quickly the rest of the characters.<br><br>I absolutely adored that we saw more of the women who live in 300 Fox Way. Maura, Calla, Persephone and Orla are just so unbelievable amazing. There’s nothing bad I can say about them and I’m more curious. Was Persephone the previous Magician? Are they going to find Blue’s father? I feel like something will happen to Calla and I can’t quite out my finger on it. I’m worried and excited with get to see more of them in the following books.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437255294ra/15559113.gif" width="500" height="205" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There wasn’t much of Blue in this book but I loved her. She was so cool and strong and she asked for more. Blue Sargent is one of the most interesting characters out there and though this wasn’t all about her, I’m dying to see how things will be next for her. <br><br>Her relationship with her mother is so unique and so right. The more I read about them, the more I love them. And now she actually acknowledged her feelings for Gansey and what she doesn’t feel about Adam, things are bound to be different.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> she very much liked the idea of it —Blue Sargent, desperado; Blue Sargent, superhero; Blue Sargent, badass.</b>
</blockquote> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443645191ra/16388688.gif" width="500" height="274" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, Gansey. <br><br>Boy, there are a lot of things going one with him. I don’t know when it’s going to appear the feeling of being the only one who’s not <i>special.</i> Like, he’s incredibly good at things, he’s a natural leader and he was the one who brought them all together and he’s a very peculiar and unique person on his own but he’s with a guy who can take things from his dreams, a ghost, a living magic increaser and a magician. I’m waiting for it, for the feeling of being left aside because I <u>feel</u> it’s going to happen eventually. Gansey’s keeping a lot of things in his heart and head, it’s going to explode someday.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403758952ra/10140560.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He’s also acknowledged his feelings for Blue, he feels guilty about them, he’s worried as fuck about Adam and he’s also relieved Ronan’s better but he’s running out of time. <br><br>Like, he’s going to die and he doesn’t know it yet and it’s killing me and Blue and I’m scared. <br><br>Now, I missed Noah. A lot. <br><br>I didn’t know I was going to miss him this much until he disappeared. I hope now Cabeswater is back and magic can be restored, he can also be back because damn, I miss him. He’s the glue, whether they know it or not, he’s the glue of the group and he and Blue are so cool together I may cry.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> “I’d ask you out, if I was alive.”<br>Nothing was fair.<br>“I’d say okay,” she replied.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Like I said, I don’t know if this one’s better than the first one. I was more frustrated in this book, that much I can say. I loved the new characters and how the old ones were explored and what about that ending? When did Maura go to Cabeswater? Is she in there? She could be in that cavern where the river was.<br><br><i>The Raven King, make way for the Raven King.</i> Gansey?<br><br>There are a lot of things that can happen in the next book and I’m so excited to read it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2168105319225821513" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1243226017" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243226017" />
    <a title="Jenny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7004681-jenny"><img alt="Jenny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376679883p2/7004681.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243226017?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny" href="/user/show/7004681-jenny">Jenny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243226017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17765102514200684777">***27. March 2016***<br/>I rarely ever reread an entire series before the release of a new book, ergo my constant sequel amnesia, but this is the <u>
  <i>Raven Cycle </i>
</u>. It's one of those books that just keeps on giving. The more you read, the more you discover. It has a really high reread factor as well because future actions shed light on past actions, turning each reread into small treasure hunts looking for those hints peppered into the story. <br/>And the characters, don't get me started on the characters.</span>
  <span id="freeText17765102514200684777" style="display:none">***27. March 2016***<br />I rarely ever reread an entire series before the release of a new book, ergo my constant sequel amnesia, but this is the <u>
  <i>Raven Cycle </i>
</u>. It's one of those books that just keeps on giving. The more you read, the more you discover. It has a really high reread factor as well because future actions shed light on past actions, turning each reread into small treasure hunts looking for those hints peppered into the story. <br />And the characters, don't get me started on the characters. Their character exploration is insane and subtle and beautiful. I know, normally I'm all about character <i>development</i>, but this wouldn't be the right word to use here. It's like Blue's tarot card, the Page of Cups. She's an empty cup brimming with potential. Our OT5 they don't grow <b>OUT</b> of their characters. They grow <b>IN</b> to their characters. Book by book they turn their potential into something real. Our characters aren't reluctant heroes who follow a certain path and are surprised to realize they've become "something more" by the end of their journey. They already <i>know</i> what their "something more" is, they know they'll reach it, they just don't know how. Yet.<br /><br />***2. April 2015***<br />First of all, a LOT happens in these book but NOT ENOUGH happens in these books. Ronan is a total bamf. Adam is finally getting his shit together. I'm still waiting for my ship to sail. I DON'T WANT TO WAIT TILL THE LAST BOOK. UNACCEPTABLE.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17765102514200684777" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2220428758" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2220428758" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2220428758?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2220428758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14031710289351862654"> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514542542ra/24788938.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> “You really didn't see the sadness or the longing unless you already knew it was there. <br/>But that was the trick, wasn't it? <br/>Everyone had their disappointment and their baggage; <br/>only, some people carried it in their inside pockets and not on their backs.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>The second book in the raven cycle is about dreams and the magic in it. <br/>It’s about things disappearing and appearing.<br/>About new enemies, friends and feelings. <br/>I was addicted from the start 😍<br/>(not surprising, I guess) <br/><br/>Characters ⭐</span>
  <span id="freeText14031710289351862654" style="display:none"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514542542ra/24788938.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “You really didn't see the sadness or the longing unless you already knew it was there. <br>But that was the trick, wasn't it? <br>Everyone had their disappointment and their baggage; <br>only, some people carried it in their inside pockets and not on their backs.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>The second book in the raven cycle is about dreams and the magic in it. <br>It’s about things disappearing and appearing.<br>About new enemies, friends and feelings. <br>I was addicted from the start 😍<br>(not surprising, I guess) <br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>The main characters stayed the same, but you get to know them better. <br>Gansey stayed my favorite, even though I learned to love Ronan a little bit (= a lot) ♥️<br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>In this World there are places that shouldn’t exist, things out of dreams and magic in people that seem absolutely normal.<br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>As in the first book the friendship between the group of boys is adorable and absolutely perfect. And they see Blue as their equal. <br>And then this tension between Gansey and Blue. Ugh, I love it. ♥️💔<br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Maggie’s Stiefvaters writing is, as usual, perfect and absolutely addictive. <br>Gimme more! <br><br>Where’s the next book? Ah, on my shelf. 🎈</span>
  <a data-text-id="14031710289351862654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4166814-bgurl-don-t-h8-me-cuz-i-m-honestful?shelf=read-reread-rereread">read-reread-rereread</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1696306764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7769404549692394804"><b><i>The Dream Thieves (RC 02)</i>, by Maggie Stiefvater: 5 “Dreams Come True” Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697251.gif' width='410' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> “A secret is a strange thing.” ~ Ronan Lynch.</i><br/><br/><b>If anyone knows about strange secrets, it’s Ronan Lynch.</b> Turns out, Richard Gansey III’s left-hand man has lots of secrets. All of them crazy. Crazy scary. Crazy unbelievable. Crazy heartbreaking. And, just plain crazy, crazy. In <i>The Dream Thieves</i>, book two of Maggie Stiefvater’s <i>Raven Cycle</i> series, we learn them all. Well, <i>almost</i> all. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697252.gif' width='410' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>“All of us have secrets in our lives.” ~ </i></span>
  <span id="freeText7769404549692394804" style="display:none"><b><i>The Dream Thieves (RC 02)</i>, by Maggie Stiefvater: 5 “Dreams Come True” Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697251.gif" width="410" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “A secret is a strange thing.” ~ Ronan Lynch.</i><br><br><b>If anyone knows about strange secrets, it’s Ronan Lynch.</b> Turns out, Richard Gansey III’s left-hand man has lots of secrets. All of them crazy. Crazy scary. Crazy unbelievable. Crazy heartbreaking. And, just plain crazy, crazy. In <i>The Dream Thieves</i>, book two of Maggie Stiefvater’s <i>Raven Cycle</i> series, we learn them all. Well, <i>almost</i> all. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697252.gif" width="410" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“All of us have secrets in our lives.” ~ Ronan Lynch.</i><br><br><b>Ronan may have the most secrets.</b> He might even have the craziest secrets. But he’s definitely not the only one with secrets. Maura and the psychics know more about Blue’s father than they’re telling. Adam (Gansey’s right-hand man) struggles to hide the repercussions of his promise to Cabeswater. Blue &amp; Gansey try to suppress their mutual attraction. And a very bad man sends an even badder man to Henrietta to find a mysterious, magical item called “The Greywaren”. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697253.gif" width="440" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Every day, thousands of confessions are kept from their would-be confessors, none of these people knowing that their never-admitted secrets all boil down to the same three words: I am afraid.” ~ Ronan Lynch.</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“I am afraid.”</i>
</b> <br><br>And, therein lies one of the main themes of, <i>The Raven Cycle</i> series. Because:<br><br>TRUTH: Everyone <i>does</i> have secrets. TRUTH: Everyone <i>is</i> afraid of something. TRUTH: The only way to overcome our fears <i>is</i> to face them. TRUTH: Maggie Stiefvater does a <i>very</i> good job of driving that point home. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468366323ra/19697254.gif" width="420" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“It’s not my job to tell other people’s secrets.” ~ Noah Czerny.</i><br><br><b>NOR IS IT MINE…</b> <br><br>If you want to know everyone's secrets, you’re going to have to read <i>The Dream Thieves</i>. Considering Ms. Stiefvater’s superior storytelling skills, that won’t be a hardship. You’ll not only love Ronan's secrets, but everyone else's as well. As for me, I’m getting ready to descend into book three. So, I’ll see y’all on the other side. ‘Til then, may you…<br><br><i>Dream on.<br>Dream on.<br>Dream until your dreams come true.<br>~ Aerosmith.</i><br><br><b>LINKS TO REVIEWS OF BOOKS 1 &amp; 3-4:</b><br><i>The Raven Boys (RC #1):</i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1692794006?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Click Me Baby!</a><br><i>Blue Lily, Lily Blue (RC #3):</i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1699966185" rel="nofollow noopener">1 More Time!</a> <br><i>The Raven King (RC #4):</i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1692242580?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">&amp; One Last Time!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7769404549692394804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6OhW7WZ5SbOi/FmHwQOa8xr33bcr/lAoRZFGIs8i5jiFm7JeXCkINX/VH2EV33lPtQQ7SJJw6oIE//ZLFoJFpQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tg7mN+kvQMQzf9rsMzZ9yiay/+QOVfOaedcrxMKtSfnbfQKE038BQu5WnArn6p52iUEZG7fbSTA4uZutGw3qZA==')})
  }
//]]>
